local k = {205, 247, 212, 60, 62, 46, 147, 125, 101, 138, 59, 79, 158, 92, 48, 85, 42, 224, 137, 109, 26, 89, 56, 186}
local a = "ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZabcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789+/"
local m = {}
for i = 1, #a do m[a:sub(i, i)] = i - 1 end
p = p:gsub("%s", "")
local e = {}
local z = 0
for i = 1, #p, 4 do
    local c1, c2 = m[p:sub(i, i)], m[p:sub(i + 1, i + 1)]
    local s3, s4 = p:sub(i + 2, i + 2), p:sub(i + 3, i + 3)
    local c3, c4 = m[s3] or 0, m[s4] or 0
    local n = c1 * 262144 + c2 * 4096 + c3 * 64 + c4
    z += 1; e[z] = math.floor(n / 65536) % 256
    if s3 ~= "=" then z += 1; e[z] = math.floor(n / 256) % 256 end
    if s4 ~= "=" then z += 1; e[z] = n % 256 end
end
local o = table.create(#e)
for i = 1, #e do o[i] = string.char(bit32.bxor(e[i], k[((i - 1) % #k) + 1])) end
local q = table.concat(o)
local h = 0
for i = 1, #q do h = (h + string.byte(q, i) * i) % 4294967291 end
if h ~= 1992883188 then error("integrity check failed") end
local f, r = loadstring(q)
if not f then error(r) end
return f()
